# STATUS вҖ” Massive Research Tool

**Last updated:** 2026-06-30
**Design language locked at v0.7 (2026-06-22):** Identity shift from warm-parchment-light-only to dark + light dual mode with intensive emerald (`#0AB667`) accent. Plex Serif retained for headlines + study titles + metric numbers; Plex Sans body. Primary CTA = white text on darker emerald (`#047144`, AAA contrast, Stripe-coded). Input default size locked at 42px / 14px text / 8px radius / hairline border (B-variant). Global search = soft-filled 44px with leading icon + вҢҳK chip. Light is default; researcher can toggle to dark per-account. v0.6 design-language brief + tokens archived to `99_archive/v06-design-language-2026-06-22/` with revert path documented. `03_design/design-language-brief.md` + `03_design/design-system/tokens.md` rewritten as v0.7 sources of truth. `05_app/styles/tokens.css` NOT yet updated вҖ” visual migration is a coordinated future handoff (would break the live v0.6-coded app if updated piecemeal). Wireframes mostly remain valid (reference layout + content + interaction patterns, not pixel-locked colors); migration pass will surface specific frames needing re-render. Memory updated (v0.6/v0.6.2 marked historical; v0.7 lock added). Figma-sync workflow still gated on owner reconnecting the Figma MCP вҖ” when green, push v0.7 tokens + components to a new "MRT Design System v0.7" file.

Per-post content + branding + reactions + comments + slots are all edited in **one place (Design вҶ’ Social)** per the owner's consolidation call; Configure shrinks to title + Save-as-reusable + a deep-link button (`?tab=social&block=<id>`) and a summary of what's set. **UX punch-list closed this pass:** (1) `block` tier suppresses chrome (ADR-0084); (2) **`layout` (inspired) now visibly differs from `branded`** вҖ” branded carries the uploaded logo + platform blue + native "Suggested for you" cue, layout keeps the structure but a neutral grey accent, no logo, no platform phrasing; (3) context-panel tabs scroll via **arrows, not a scrollbar** (`ScrollableTabs`); (4) Design tabs hide when the study has no Chat/Social blocks; (5) "Needs setup" fixed (source no longer required); (6) reactions selectable + comments likeable + author/comment avatars uploadable; (7) the deferred **`reaction` export column** now ships (one analyzable `*_reaction` column per social-post block). Opening Preview calls the runtime `openRecruitment` on the DRAFT version + writes a `mode:"preview"` response, so a previewed-but-never-run study showed Recruiting вң“ / Data in вң“ / Recruitment Open / "Completed responses: 1" + a phantom "Opened recruitment" changelog line вҖ” while Run/Results (which require a frozen runnable version) correctly said it wasn't running. Fixed by restricting every *real-data* read to `mode:"run"` responses + recruitment on frozen runnable versions: `studyDashboard` (counts, recruitment, condition balance), `changelog` recruitment entries, the finish-info query, the `setFinished` precondition (a preview could otherwise satisfy "collect вүҘ1 response"), the public study-record N, and the admin census. me/workspace/dashboard.ts already filtered. +1 regression test (892 total). tsc/lint/build/validator clean. **No migration. Round 5g вҖ” owner corrections (committed, unpushed; no migration):** **(post content font now STATIC)** reverted the 5e change that made the FB post headline/body scale with the study font setting вҖ” owner wants post copy to always render at the same default size; back to fixed 15px (FB-native), like the rest of the post chrome (the study font-size setting still drives general study text on other blocks via `--text-*`, just not the social-post copy). **(Like-icon size consistency вҖ” root cause)** the post's Like affordance had paths at two sizes: `ReactionButton` + the *live* `ReactionPicker` trigger inherit the action bar's 16px, but the `ReactionPicker` **inert/display-only paths hardcoded `text-[13px]`**, so a post with reactions set display-only (`reactionsLive=false`) rendered the Like at 13px while an interactive one rendered 16px вҖ” same post, two sizes. Dropped the hardcoded sizes so every Like path inherits the action bar size (one consistent size). **(comment count coherence)** "View more comments" now only renders when the post's comment count actually exceeds the seeded comments on display (`e.comments > seeded.length`); previously it always showed, implying hidden comments that don't exist when all were already visible. 895 tests; tsc/lint/build/validator (252) clean. **DEPLOYED 4251d80. Server `getResults` emits `spshared:`/`spcomment:`/`spreplies:` keys next to `reaction:`; dataset.ts omits the packed column for social-post and emits the split set; +2 export tests (896 total). tsc/lint/build/validator clean. **(2 + 5 вҖ” social-post conditioning, DONE вҖ” owner: branch on reaction only):** the condition builder's free-text value box for a social-post source is now a **dropdown of the 7 reactions** (Like/Love/Care/Haha/Wow/Sad/Angry). `operatorsForKey("social-post")` вҶ’ single-select operators (is / is not / is any of + "is answered" = reacted at all); `answerValues` recognizes a social-post answer (liked+shared boolean pair) and returns the chosen `reaction` (empty when none, so "is answered" reads as "reacted"); `isConditionSource` now includes social-post and excludes pure stimuli (text/image/video/audio/link). Runtime evaluates against the raw answer object (`answersFor` returns JSON), so "reaction is Wow" branches correctly. +2 condition tests (898 total). tsc/lint/build/validator clean. **DEPLOYED 1bc4bf1. Round 5j вҖ” restore didn't clear the drift banner (committed, unpushed; no migration):** owner restored Published v1 but the "draft has changes that aren't live" banner + "draft ahead" pill stayed. **Two root causes:** (1) `restoreVersion` was a **partial restore** вҖ” `writeBlocks` does `{...prev, blocks}`, so it only overwrote the draft's blocks and left theme/consent/overview/groups/variants **and conditions** untouched; but `divergedFromLive` fingerprints the **full snapshot + conditions**, so any non-block divergence kept drift on forever. Now restore copies the **whole snapshot verbatim + replaces the draft's conditions** with the restored version's (transaction), so the tip becomes byte-identical and the fingerprint matches вҶ’ drift genuinely clears. (2) The banner/pill read `getRunInfo`, which was **never invalidated** on restore (or on any builder edit) вҖ” added `getRunInfo` invalidation to the restore success handler AND the builder's shared `invalidate()`, so the banner refreshes immediately. +1 integration test (restore clears drift after a block **and** a condition edit вҖ” the blocks-only path would fail it). 899 tests; tsc/lint/build/validator clean. **DEPLOYED 66c4238. Round 5k вҖ” Activity "Yours" feed frozen since ~June 22 (committed, unpushed; no migration):** owner-authorized read-only prod query confirmed it: `activity_event` had 44 rows (latest Jun 30) but `notification` only 8 (latest **Jun 22 06:20**) вҖ” activity WAS being logged, but the **`notification.fanout` job stopped running**. Root cause: fan-out was an Inngest-queued job; Inngest Cloud stopped invoking the `/api/inngest` callback (app-sync/keys lapsed after a deploy), and `emit()`'s inline fallback only fires in dev вҖ” so in prod events kept logging while notifications silently stopped. **Fix:** `emit()` now runs `runNotificationFanout` **inline** (idempotent via `UNIQUE(recipient, source_event)`), removing the fragile queue dependency for this critical path; best-effort try/catch so a fan-out error never fails the triggering action. Updated 4 fan-out tests (emit/comments/notifications/registry-push) to assert inline delivery + that `notification.fanout` is no longer enqueued. 900 tests; tsc/lint/build/validator clean. DEPLOYED 3a63461. **CORRECTION after backfill (owner-authorized prod run):** the one-off backfill re-ran fan-out over ALL 36 activity_events lacking a notification and added **0** вҖ” so the `notification` table is fully consistent with `activity_event`; **nothing was lost**, and the "Inngest fan-out is broken" hypothesis is NOT supported. The "Yours" feed only surfaces notifications *to* you (comments, mentions, reviews, a replication *of your* study, or an OSF-registration push completing = "Your preregistration is live" via `osf_push_complete`). The recent events (template_used, fork of own/starter, non-OSF preregister вҖ” all follows-only/actor-only) correctly generate no personal notification, so the feed is legitimately quiet since 16.06. The inline-fan-out change is **kept as hardening** (removes the Inngest single-point-of-failure for the notification path) but was NOT the cause. Inngest health for the remaining jobs (registry.push OSF pushes, recruitment reconcile) is unverified from here вҖ” owner can confirm in the Inngest dashboard; a stuck OSF push would be the real symptom of an Inngest outage. Backfill + diagnostic scripts removed after use. **Round 5l вҖ” personal dashboard replication widgets (committed, unpushed; no migration):** two new `/home` widgets (owner asked for both directions): **"Studies you replicated"** (`your-replications` вҖ” your forks across workspaces, each linking back to the original) and **"Replications of your studies"** (`replications-of-mine` вҖ” others replicating your work: who + which study + when; informational, no link since the fork is private). Two `meRouter` procedures (`myReplications`, `replicationsOfMine`) over the existing fork graph (no schema change), added to `WIDGET_REGISTRY` + the user default layout, wired into home-widgets + home/page. +1 me integration test (both directions via a real fork). 901 tests; tsc/lint/build/validator clean. **Still queued (bigger, needs a gate):** the cross-workspace notification center in the top nav вҖ” global **What's New** (the existing вңЁ announcements bell, already user-level via `last_seen_announcement_at`) + a global **Activity** entry aggregating across workspaces + flagging "something new." **Next:** deploy the widgets; then scope the notification-center with a wireframe/ADR.

(3) **Duplicate profile bio** (01KW5CKK part) вҖ” removed the bio field from AccountвҶ’Profile; the Public-profile section is now the single bio editor. (Per-study replication count already hidden when 0 on /u/<handle>.) (4) **Wording editor** (01KW4S698, already deployed 4323afd) вҖ” block groups show only for blocks in the study. **Feedback status control already exists + works** in /admin/feedback (the `setStatus` select) вҖ” usable as a task board now; a raw prod status write from the agent is (correctly) classifier-blocked, so the owner flips statuses there. 832 tests; tsc/lint/build clean. Code-only. **Remaining feedback (queued, owner to prioritise / some need scope):** template preview on /browse (01KW4PSR), richer changelog + detail filter (01KW4R8M), tour feedback button + annotated screenshots (01KW4SHRT), profile avatars + articles (01KW5CKK rest вҖ” avatar upload deferred; "articles" undefined), dashboard "why use it" value-prop (01KW4HMV).

**Prior focus (2026-06-28):** **Hotfix вҖ” admin metrics dashboard resilience (ADR-0080).** Prod showed "Couldn't load metrics" on /admin (the whole `admin.metrics` query 500'd while the server-rendered census tiles loaded). Root-caused to the metrics resolver having no failure isolation вҖ” any single failing piece (the `admin_metric_snapshot` cache read/write or an external adapter) rejected the whole Promise.all. Fix: `resolveCachedMetric` now wraps its entire body in try/catch (degrades to `{available:false}` вҖ” a missing snapshot table or DB hiccup can no longer break the page), and the resolver splits DB metrics (own try/catch вҶ’ zeros + a surfaced `dbError`) from the now-safe external calls, so the dashboard ALWAYS renders whatever succeeded. `<AdminMetrics>` surfaces `dbError` if present. Migrations 0048/0049 re-applied to prod (idempotent) in case 0048 hadn't landed. +1 test (cache never throws on a throwing fetcher). 828 tests; tsc/lint/build clean. Code-only (no migration). Deployed. **Follow-up (same day):** the surfaced `dbError` was the real bug вҖ” postgres-js rejects a raw JS `Date` interpolated into a `sql\`\` FILTER expression ("Received an instance of Date"; pglite tolerated it so tests passed). Fixed by interpolating ISO strings with `::timestamptz` casts on all five date thresholds. Also reorganized the dashboard per owner feedback (it "looked messy"): the navigational queue tiles (Workspaces/Feedback/Announcements) now sit at the TOP, then the live DB sections (Growth / Studies & responses / AI cost), then clearly-named **PostHog В· product analytics** and **Sentry В· error monitoring** sections (active users + active-user-vs-events no longer mixed into Growth). Deployed.

(Found independently by the hot-spot-actions design workflow вҶ’ its `setValue` tags fold into the answer payload, not response metadata.) Not yet surfaced in the export вҖ” a follow-up if wanted.

**Earlier (2026-06-03):** **Step 3 began вҖ” the OSF registration push is now REAL (adapter), verified against OSF's own swagger + backend serializer.** `registry.osf.ts pushRegistration` implements the verified 4-call JSON:API flow: `POST /v2/nodes/` вҶ’ `POST /nodes/{id}/draft_registrations/` (schema resolved by name, default "Open-Ended Registration") вҶ’ `PATCH /draft_registrations/{id}/` (registration_responses.summary = human text + lossless JSON snapshot) вҶ’ `POST /nodes/{id}/registrations/` (`draft_registration` + `registration_choice:"immediate"`). **Key finding: the DOI is async** вҖ” OSF's `RegistrationCreateSerializer.create()` calls `require_approval()`, so a fresh registration is pending-approval and the DOI mints on approval. `PushResult` changed to `{registrationId, url, doi: string|null}` (URL immediate, DOI backfilled). ADR-0005 amended with the verified flow + DOI-async + the Open-Ended schema choice (why-not OSF Preregistration: many required structured fields вҶ’ V1.6). Amendment/withdrawal stay NOT_IMPLEMENTED (V1.6). **STEP 3 COMPLETE вҖ” Preregister stage works end to end. 67 vitest green; typecheck + build + validator clean.** Backend: the **`registry.push` Inngest job** (`server/jobs/registry-push.ts` вҖ” plain async body, PGlite-tested; records a `registry_push` attempt, calls the adapter, writes outcome to the attempt row + version push-status; `no_credentials` terminal, transient errors rethrow) registered in `/api/inngest`; the **`studies.preregister` mutation** (immutable `kind:preregistered` snapshot вҶ’ connected вҮ’ `pending` + enqueue, else `no_credentials`); the **`studies.getPreregistration` query** (latest preregistered version + push status). UI: the **Preregister-stage wireframe spec** (design gate cleared, 10 wireframes) + the **`/studies/[id]/preregister` route** (RSC: header + OSF connection chip + Preregister action / push-status receipt banner per state) + **StageTabs** now activates Build **and** Preregister. Also added **`studies.retryPush` + a Retry-push button** (preregister page, `failed`/`no_credentials` states) so a push can be recovered without creating a new version вҖ” re-pushes the same frozen snapshot. **Live OSF test result:** the push reached OSF and returned **403 on `POST /nodes/` ("not authorized to this view")** вҖ” a token-scope issue (a read-only PAT connects fine via `GET /users/me/` but can't create nodes); fix is a write-scoped (`osf.full_write`) token + reconnect, then Retry push. **Known follow-up:** harden `connectWithToken` to detect a non-write token at connect time (immediate error vs silent failure at push). **Next: step 4 вҖ” participant runtime (ADR-0013): server-rendered MPA `/take/[studyId]/[sessionId]/[questionIndex]` + Preview (`?preview=true`)**, then step 5 Run (recruitment URL), step 6 Results + CSV, plus the failing-first Hanna-runtime e2e (preregister вҶ’ recruit вҶ’ complete вҶ’ 1 response вҶ’ aggregate).

**Earlier (2026-06-03):** **OSF connect unblocked via Personal Access Token (ADR-0005 amendment).** Live OAuth on localhost is dead-ended: OSF's CAS rejects a `localhost` redirect (matching `http://localhost` callback вҶ’ `invalid_client`; `https://localhost` вҶ’ "invalid request parameters" at OSF's redirect-validation step вҖ” our authorize request is provably well-formed). Verified by serving over https (self-signed openssl cert, `npm run dev:https`) and probing OSF's authorize endpoint directly. Also fixed a real latent bug: `TOKEN_ENCRYPTION_KEY` is hex but `crypto/tokens.ts` only decoded base64 вҶ’ would throw at the callback (`getKey` now accepts hex or base64). **Decision (owner-approved): add a PAT connect path** вҖ” paste an `osf.full_write` token from `osf.io/settings/tokens` in Account Settings В· Connections; validated against `GET /v2/users/me/`, stored encrypted in the same `registry_connection` row as an OAuth token; `RegistryAdapter.connectWithToken` is the one additive method. OAuth stays for a future deployed https domain. **This is the only path that can drive the automated Hanna e2e** (OAuth needs interactive login). **59 vitest green; typecheck clean.** **Next (step 3):** Preregister stage вҖ” immutable `kind:preregistered` version + enqueue the `registry.push` Inngest job (implements the OSF push) + DOI/status banner. Then steps 4-6 (runtime/Preview вҶ’ Run вҶ’ Results) + the failing-first Hanna-runtime e2e.

Final piece: `e2e/hanna-loop.spec.ts` (`@clerk/testing`) drives sign-in вҶ’ from-Framework вҶ’ configure вҶ’ save named вҶ’ reopen-persists, **gated behind `RUN_AUTH_E2E=1`** (skips in this sandbox вҖ” no Clerk CDN вҖ” runs on your machine/CI). **Verified: 50 vitest + 4 surface e2e green (loop e2e skipped), typecheck + build clean.** The loop e2e itself is **unverified** (sign-in strategy/selectors best-effort). **To close V1-MVP:** run the loop e2e green on a real Clerk instance + a manual live click-through of block editing & save, then a QA audit-log entry.

**Earlier (2026-06-02):** **ADR-0011 MVP authoring loop works on Blank + from-Framework paths (Framework registry).** Shipped the Misinformation Research Framework as an **in-repo curated definition** (`server/frameworks/registry.ts`: social-post stimulus + pre-worded likert-7 manipulation check); DB-backed `Framework`/`FrameworkVersion` deferred to curator authoring (`data-model/03-framework-entities.md`). `frameworks.list` feeds the New-study modal's Framework picker (enabled); `studies.create({kind:"framework"})` copies the framework's blocks into the new study's autosave (fresh ULIDs, preset configs, locks derived per ADR-0012). **QA: 50 vitest + 4 e2e green, typecheck + build clean.** **Remaining for full MVP:** the **full Hanna-loop e2e** (`@clerk/testing`, env-gated вҖ” skips in this sandbox, green on your machine/CI).

**Earlier (2026-06-02):** **ADR-0011 MVP authoring loop code-complete (Blank path) вҖ” Save-as-version dialog.** Signup вҶ’ onboard вҶ’ `/studies` вҶ’ New study вҶ’ Builder (add + configure blocks, autosaved) вҶ’ **Save as named version**. The Save-as-version dialog landed (`save-as-version-dialog.md`): `studies.saveAsNamed` snapshots the autosave working tip into a new immutable `named` ExperimentVersion (label-unique, next version_number) per ADR-0012, autosave continues; dialog offers autosave / named (default) / review-deferred, advisory (non-blocking) warning for incomplete blocks, saved toast. **QA: 48 vitest + 4 e2e green, typecheck + build clean.** **Remaining for full MVP:** the full **Hanna-loop e2e** (`@clerk/testing` вҖ” green on your machine, not this sandbox) and the **Misinformation Research Framework seed** (item 9, unlocks the "from Framework" start). Block editing + save are test-covered but not yet clicked in a real browser.

## Overall

- Artifacts done: 25 Foundation + 14 Product + 11 Architecture + 4 Research + 14 Design = 68 (+ 2 Build commits)
- **Open quality compromise (logged honestly):** all four personas rest on synthetic-pilot evidence + literature, not field interviews. Confidence is `medium` for the literature-validated claims, `low` for the segmentation-specific claims. Each persona's "Open questions / what to validate" section names specific revisit triggers вҖ” most are "before V1 ships" or "before any high-stakes design decision depending on this persona."
- Active phase: Product (Phase 2) + Architecture (Phase 4) + Research (Phase 1) running in parallel
- Positioning RESOLVED: Qualtrics + GitHub for research, combined.
- Module architecture RESOLVED: versioned modular composition with theme overlays (ADR-0001).
- Forking model RESOLVED: snapshot-based, pull-from-upstream deferred but forward-ready (ADR-0002).
- **Persona evidence base STRENGTHENED**: literature confirms tool fragmentation, OSF integration as credibility floor, misinformation-tooling demand, and Prolific dominance for recruiting; some persona claims (modern-UX-as-credibility, "computing-power" specifics) still need interview confirmation.

## Phase 3 вҖ” Design

Started 2026-05-28; advancing.

- Inspiration вҶ’ `03_design/inspiration/`
  - `README.md` вҖ” intake convention.
  - `2026-05-28-first-batch.md` вҖ” six annotated references (Maze, Notion, TheyDo, Typeform Build/Logic/Modal); three-zone layout pattern, builder-vs-whiteboard duality, right-drawer + live-preview combinations.
- `design-language-brief.md` вҖ” **v0.5.3**. Stage-tabs placement re-locked from Option A (v0.5.2 Typeform pattern, top-bar center slot) to **Option B (Miro / FigJam pattern, floating pill above center work surface only)** after the project owner saw both in context. Better matches the brief's modular-floating-panels spirit: top bar stays slim with global chrome only (workspace + breadcrumb left; вҢҳK + Save when on a study + user avatar right); stage-tabs pill spans only the center column width and floats over the work surface card it controls; side rails extend full height of the center column. Three modules on a parchment board with a slim top hat вҖ” clean modular reading. Layout system + Top-bar navigation sections rewritten. Build-stage-builder-mode wireframe spec updated to match. All v0.5.1 commitments (warm parchment, modular panels, Plex Serif promotion, Light/Dark with full token tables, Themeability) preserved.
- *(superseded v0.5.1 description retained in changelog of `design-language-brief.md`.)* IBM Plex Serif/Sans/Mono locked. Three refinements to v0.5: (a) parchment paled вҖ” `surface.page #F4EFE6 вҶ’ #F7F2E8`, `surface.panel #FBF7EE вҶ’ #FCFAF3` after project-owner feedback "too creamy"; final tone held open for confirmation alongside first wireframes; (b) **dark mode upgraded from post-V1 to V1 ship** вҖ” Light + Dark + System (auto) all available with user toggle persisted per user; every neutral / border token now has Light + Dark values (dark surfaces are warm-dark, not cool slate, to preserve editorial tone); (c) **Themeability section added** вҖ” tokens are CSS variables, themes are bundles of token values, Light + Dark + System for users, internal exploration themes for design discipline (live in `03_design/design-system/themes/`, never reach production, dev-mode switch). Hard rules: no raw hex in components, every new color decision adds both Light and Dark values in the same change, every screen contrast-checked in both modes before handoff. Possible ADR-0010 (theming system) flagged but deferred until Build вҖ” implementation is straightforward (CSS vars + ThemeProvider + persisted user pref). v0.5 modular floating panels + Plex Serif in more roles + v0.4 functional vibrancy all preserved.
- Wireframes вҶ’ `03_design/wireframes/`
  - `studies-destination.md` вҖ” Hanna's home base; list of studies, sub-nav, `+ New study` entry. Draft.
  - `new-study-modal.md` вҖ” first decision point (Framework / Template / Blank). Draft.
  - `build-stage-builder-mode.md` вҖ” the meat; full three-zone modular surface with stage tabs, study title in Plex Serif, block list with status badges, right context panel tabs. Draft.
  - `save-as-version-dialog.md` вҖ” third decision point (Continue autosaving / Save as named / Save & request review). Draft.
- `ia/information-architecture.md` вҖ” **v0.3** with five new conceptual picks locked (on top of v0.2 picks). (1) **Forks live as a relationship, not a destination** вҖ” surface in three places: forker's Studies list with `Replicating {parent-author} В· {parent-study}@v` subtitle + new `Replicating` sub-nav, parent's right-panel `Replications` tab (two-directional family tree, renamed from "Lineage"), Activity stream events. No top-level "Forks" left-rail destination. (2) **Templates revoked as a Frameworks alias** вҖ” they're different concepts. Templates moves to `Library В· Templates` as its own sub-section; Frameworks stays top-level as curated systems (schema + modules + measurement + reporting conventions for a research tradition like "Misinformation Research Framework"). (3) **Activity gets a `Yours / Follows` split** вҖ” Follows is the retention surface, fed by five follow targets: tag, author, Framework, study, saved search; `+ Follow` affordance on every tag chip, author byline, Framework details tab, study details tab, and inside the search modal. (4) **Participants destination structured as five sub-views** вҖ” Panels (saved cohorts, anon IDs), Open recruitment (provider status via RegistryAdapter), Compensation (payouts/invoices), Quality (flagged sessions awaiting decision), Connections (provider OAuth). Aggregated only; PII never surfaces. (5) **Template share scopes** вҖ” four scopes (Public-replicable default per ADR-0002 / Workspace / Invite link / Submit to Framework); single `Share` panel per saved version, no multi-step publish wizard. v0.2 picks still apply (Linear workspace switcher, scoped global search, comments on both surfaces, no bell, six stages with Preregister as its own). Object-typed right-panel tab system. Builder/Whiteboard toggle in study top-bar. Studies flat (tags do grouping). Mobile collapses rail to bottom tab bar; whiteboard read-only on mobile.
- Wireframes, design system, prototypes, handoff вҶ’ next.

## Phase 4 вҖ” Architecture

Started (parallel to Product Phase 2).

- ADRs вҶ’ `04_architecture/adrs/`
  - **`0001-modular-composition-theme-overlays.md` вҖ” accepted 2026-05-27.** Versioned module identity (`source/key@version`), first-class schemas, pure-functional theme overlays, fork-version-locking, plugin-ready data model. Question-type granularity for modules.
  - **`0002-forking-model.md` вҖ” accepted 2026-05-27.** Stripped Option B: snapshot-based forking, pull-from-upstream deferred. Versions are immutable with kinds (autosave, named, preregistered, published). Forks reference a specific parent version. Participant data never copied. Public-forkable default. Frameworks share the model. Forward-readiness checklist for upgrade to full B.
  - **`0003-asset-storage.md` вҖ” accepted 2026-05-28.** Option B: hybrid (researcher choice per asset between internal R2 upload and external link), auto-freeze on preregistration/publication with per-asset opt-out, failed freezes flag the version honestly. Per-tenant storage metering architected; pricing model deferred. Content-hash dedup for internal assets.
  - **`0004-preregistration-amendments.md` вҖ” accepted 2026-05-28.** Amendments to preregistered versions follow OSF / ClinicalTrials.gov convention: a new `kind: preregistered` version with `supersedes_version_id` + required `change_summary`. Both versions remain public, immutable, queryable. No silent edits. New fields added to ExperimentVersion in the data-model entry.
  - **`0005-osf-integration.md` вҖ” accepted 2026-05-28.** Push-to-OSF on preregistration. Option B sub-B.3: JSON snapshot + rendered PDF + OSF template-field mapping + materials, pushed asynchronously via Inngest. OAuth per-user (researchers own their OSF identity), default-on with per-registration opt-out, async with retry, failed pushes flag the version honestly (never block preregistration). **Registry-agnostic adapter interface** so AsPredicted / ClinicalTrials.gov / etc. plug in later via the same shape. Three new entities sketched (Registry, RegistryConnection, RegistryPush).
  - **`0006-ai-plugin-architecture.md` вҖ” accepted 2026-05-28.** Task-based AI architecture with AIProviderAdapters (mirrors RegistryAdapter from ADR-0005). Schemas-first output validation directly enabled by ADR-0001 module schemas. Per-tenant routing with sensitivity-aware policy enforcement (`metadata_only` / `experiment_definition` / `participant_data` / `pii`). Append-only `ai_invocation` audit log + per-tenant cost metering. Caching for deterministic tasks. Human-in-the-loop UX default. V1 ships substrate only; no AI features. Four new entities sketched.
  - **`0007-path-a-vs-b.md` вҖ” accepted 2026-05-28.** Path A with adapter discipline. Vercel + Clerk + Liveblocks + Inngest; each behind a typed adapter (`HostingShape` / `AuthAdapter` / `RealtimeAdapter` / `BackgroundJobAdapter`). No vendor-specific types in application code; no Clerk pre-built UI components in production; lock-in inventory + code-review rule enforce the discipline. Cost-ceiling triggers committed: $200/mo plan, $500/mo execute per-piece. Migration order when triggered: Clerk вҶ’ Auth.js, then Liveblocks вҶ’ Yjs, then Inngest вҶ’ BullMQ, hosting last.
  - **`0009-supply-side-strategy.md` вҖ” accepted 2026-05-28.** Three-layer hybrid addressing the biggest non-technical risk. Layer 1 (now, mostly done): default virtue as continuous architectural posture вҖ” every UX decision should make the path of least resistance produce a better-documented artifact. Layer 2 (V1 GTM): demand-first targeting consortia, replicators, open-science labs; explicitly NOT trying to convert reluctant authors. Layer 3 (V2+ partnerships): mandate leverage via selected journals (Royal Society Open Science, BMJ titles, PLOS) and funders (NIH, NSF, Wellcome, DFG); gated by V1 product evidence. Back catalogue is explicitly out of scope вҖ” flow > stock.
  - **Up next:** the architecture queue is substantively complete (9 ADRs). Phase 3 (Design) is fully unblocked. ADR-0008 (plugin model, deferred from ADR-0001) is queued but not blocking.
  - Queued: `0008-plugin-model` (deferred).
- Diagrams вҶ’ `04_architecture/diagrams/` (none standalone; Mermaid ER diagrams embedded in `data-model/00-core-entities.md`)
- Data model entries вҶ’ `04_architecture/data-model/`
  - `00-core-entities.md` вҖ” Module, ModuleVersion, Theme, Experiment, ExperimentVersion + Framework note + Fork-as-relationship. Sketch, not migration. Resolves 5 ADR contradictions.
  - `04-response-conditioning-entities.md` + `05-registry-integration.md` вҖ” **added 2026-06-02 (V1.5).** The response/conditioning tables (ADR-0014) + registry-integration tables (ADR-0005); landed as migration `0002`.
  - `01-auth-tenancy-entities.md` вҖ” **added 2026-06-01.** Resolves the auth/tenancy deferral from `00-core-entities.md`. User / Workspace / Member; locks "Workspace IS the tenant" (sketch's `tenant_id` вҶ’ `workspace.id`); Clerk identity-only, membership in our DB not Clerk Orgs (ADR-0007); `hasCompletedOnboarding`/theme/lastWorkspace in Clerk `publicMetadata`, not columns. Grounds the first Drizzle migration (commit 2).
- API contracts вҶ’ `04_architecture/api-contracts/` (none yet)

## Phase 5 вҖ” Build

**Started 2026-05-29.** Scaffolded per [ADR-0011](../04_architecture/adrs/0011-scaffold-strategy.md).

- `05_app/` вҖ” Next.js 15 + React 19 + TypeScript + Tailwind v4. First commit lands the app skeleton + the full v0.6 token system + a working theme toggle + a verification page exercising every visual primitive (parchment, Plex Serif, modular cards, vibrant validation badges, three-card theme picker). Second commit lands the AuthAdapter discipline before Clerk wires. See `05_app/README.md` for install + run.
  - `app/layout.tsx` вҖ” wraps everything in `ThemeProvider`; loads IBM Plex Sans/Serif/Mono via `next/font/google`.
  - `app/page.tsx` вҖ” temporary verification page; goes away once `/studies` becomes the default landing.
  - `app/globals.css` вҖ” Tailwind v4 + `@theme inline` bridge exposing every token as a utility class; `@custom-variant dark` driven by `[data-theme="dark"]`.
  - `styles/tokens.css` вҖ” canonical Light + Dark CSS variables; 1:1 with `03_design/design-system/tokens.md`.
  - `components/theme-provider.tsx` вҖ” three-mode picker (light/dark/system), localStorage today + Clerk metadata next iteration, listens for OS theme changes when `system` is active.
  - `components/theme-toggle.tsx` вҖ” three-card picker UI matching `signup-onboarding` + `account-settings` wireframes.
  - `lib/utils.ts` вҖ” `cn()` helper.
  - `server/adapters/auth.ts` вҖ” typed `AuthAdapter` interface; identity primitives only; theme + last-workspace via narrow `AuthUserMetadata`; `Proxy` default export throws until `auth.clerk.ts` lands next commit.
  - `server/adapters/README.md` вҖ” the rule: vendor SDK imports live in this folder only; PR review enforces.
  - `components.json` (shadcn-cli config), `.env.example`, `.gitignore`, `package.json`, `tsconfig.json`, `next.config.ts`, `postcss.config.mjs`.
- `04_architecture/lock-in-inventory.md` вҖ” per-vendor breakdown (Clerk, Vercel, Liveblocks, Inngest, OSF, AI providers) with what's behind the adapter, deliberate exceptions, migration target, and cost-ceiling trigger. PR review consults this file when touching adapters.
- ADR-0007 amended 2026-05-29: Clerk migration target shifts from Auth.js вҶ’ **Better Auth** (TypeScript-first, organizations primitive built in, first-class Drizzle integration). All other terms (cost ceilings, migration order, adapter discipline) unchanged.
- **Data layer (commit 2, 2026-06-02):** `05_app/server/db/` вҖ” `schema.ts` (Drizzle: `user`/`workspace`/`member`/`experiment`/`experiment_version` + 5 enums + CHECKs from the data model + unique indexes), `client.ts` (Drizzle over **postgres-js**, `prepare:false` вҖ” interactive transactions, not `neon-http`), `migrations/0000_quiet_vampiro.sql` (generated by drizzle-kit, **applied to Neon**), `__tests__/migration.test.ts` (hermetic pglite, 9 green). `drizzle.config.ts` loads `.env.local`. Scripts: `db:generate` / `db:migrate` / `test`.

Routers `workspace.active` + `studies.list` (tenant-scoped; stage from current version kind; sub-nav filters). Consumed via an in-process RSC caller (`server/trpc/server.ts`) + an `/api/trpc` fetch handler. zod inputs. 7 router tests (scoping + guards); 34 vitest total green. Deps: `@trpc/server` v11, `zod`.
- **Signup onboarding (commit 4, 2026-06-02):** `05_app/app/(auth)/` вҖ” `layout.tsx` (centered parchment column) + custom `signup`/`signin`/`signup/verify`/`signup/sso-callback` pages (no Clerk prebuilt UI; magic-link via `createEmailLinkFlow`, Google via `authenticateWithRedirect`, callbacks via the headless `handleEmailLinkVerification`/`handleRedirectCallback` hooks). `server/onboarding/finalize.ts` (one `postgres-js` transaction: user upsert + workspace + owner member; metadata via adapter). `app/actions/set-theme.ts` (durable theme persist); `ThemeProvider` extended (Clerk-free) + `ThemeToggle` arrow-key nav; `app/page.tsx` authenticated welcome. `e2e/signup-slice.spec.ts` + `playwright.config.ts` (3 green). **`@clerk/nextjs` pinned to v6.39.5** (v7.4.x's new signals API diverges from the documented classic hooks). 27 vitest + 3 e2e green; typecheck + build clean.

## Suggested next moves

1. **Create GitHub repo + add remote + push baseline.** On your end: create an empty private repo at `github.com/<your-username>/massive-research-tool` (no README/license/.gitignore вҖ” we have those). Then run from the project root:
   ```bash
   cd "/Users/pawelrosner/Dropbox/Mac/Documents/Claude/Projects/Massive Research Tool"
   git remote add origin git@github.com:<your-username>/massive-research-tool.git
   git push -u origin main
   ```
   (Use the HTTPS URL `https://github.com/...` instead if you don't have SSH set up. The first push asks you to authenticate.)
2. **Switch to Code tab in the Claude desktop app.** Pre-paste your `.env.local` with Clerk publishable key + secret key + Neon `DATABASE_URL`. Then start the session with: *"Continue from STATUS.md. Next move is the Clerk + Drizzle + signup commit per ADR-0011 step 2. Keys are in 05_app/.env.local."*
3. **Set up Playwright + write the failing MVP e2e first** per `qa-and-testing.md`. Single spec covers Hanna's whole loop: signup вҶ’ study from Framework вҶ’ 2 blocks вҶ’ Save as named version вҶ’ return tomorrow, find draft.
4. **Build the Studies destination** once the failing e2e exists. tRPC `studies.list` router + Drizzle query + the three-zone modular layout per `studies-destination.md` wireframe.
5. **Then in order**: New study modal вҶ’ Builder mode (one block) вҶ’ Module picker popover вҶ’ Save dialog. Each gated by an e2e assertion. Misinformation Research Framework seeded with two starter blocks.
6. **Post-MVP wireframes (V1.5+)** deferred: Whiteboard mode, Replications tab populated, Activity Yours/Follows, Preregister stage, Share stage, Run stage, Results stage, Participants five sub-views, Team destination.
7. **Open IA questions queued** вҖ” cross-workspace participant registry, AI features home (Settings В· AI), follow-target notification cadence (Settings В· Notifications). Resolve when MVP-adjacent surfaces are built.
8. **ADR-0008 (plugin model)** вҖ” deferred architectural ADR. Wait for a real third-party plugin author to design for.
9. **ADR-0012 candidate (participant runtime + 3rd-party analytics)** вҖ” surfaced 2026-05-29 by project-owner question about Clarity / heatmap support. Researcher-facing app is SPA-like (fine вҖ” no third-party analytics on admin surfaces). Participant runtime is deferred to V1.5 per ADR-0011; when we design it, **build as server-rendered multi-page navigation** вҖ” `/take/[studyId]/[questionIndex]` per-question routes, real page transitions, no SPA on the participant side вҖ” so researchers can use Microsoft Clarity / Hotjar / FullStory / PostHog cleanly (same reason Qualtrics + SurveyMonkey render survey responses page-by-page). Add a researcher settings page to paste a third-party tracking ID; server-inject the script only on `/take/*` routes, never on the dashboard. GDPR consent flow for participant tracking needs product-level resolution. Don't write the ADR yet вҖ” design properly when V1.5 participant work starts.

- **2026-06-27** вҖ” **fix(admin): workspace census all-zeroes + feedback triage actions + PostHog/Sentry links (owner-flagged).** Three issues the owner caught on the live admin: (1) **Census bug** вҖ” `/admin/workspaces` showed 0 members + 0 studies for every workspace despite real data; the correlated-subquery counts (`(select count(*) вҖҰ where m.workspace_id = ${workspace.id})`) silently bound the interpolated outer column to the inner table, always returning 0. - **2026-06-27** вҖ” **feat: AA1.2b вҖ” server-readable consent cookie (ADR-0073 amendment 1).** Closes the consent-propagation gap from AA1.2 (owner chose the cookie approach). The cookie banner now mirrors the choice into a **non-httpOnly, non-sensitive `cookie_consent` cookie** (coarse `all`/`necessary` only вҖ” no PII; `Path=/`, `SameSite=Lax`, 1-year, `Secure` on https), written on every choice **and backfilled on mount** for returning users. `getServerConsent` resolves **cookie вҶ’ newest `cookie_consent` row вҶ’ "necessary"**, so server-side analytics now honours consent reliably (localStorage was invisible to the server, and audit rows are usually keyed by `pre_signup_id` not `user_id`). New `writeConsentCookie` helper in `lib/legal/cookie-consent.ts`. +1 test (cookie preferred over DB). 793 tests; tsc/lint/build/validator clean. No migration. **Unblocks AA1.3** (wiring the remaining ~30 taxonomy events).
- **2026-06-27** вҖ” **feat: AA1.2 вҖ” server analytics seam (`AnalyticsAdapter` + PostHog, ADR-0074).** The server half of analytics, behind an adapter (ADR-0007). New **`server/adapters/analytics.ts`** (interface + strict `AnalyticsEvent` taxonomy, ~31 events, + `SensitivityTag` that deliberately omits `pii`/`participant_data`) and **`analytics.posthog.ts`** вҖ” the only `posthog-node` importer: hard no-op unless a key is set, **consent no-op** (anything but "all"), **sensitivity guard** (a forbidden tag THROWS so misuse surfaces loudly, ADR-0014), per-workspace **group** rollup, and **serverless flush** (flushAt 1 + awaited `flush()` so events survive function freeze). **`getServerConsent(userId)`** reads the newest `cookie_consent` row (defaults "necessary" вҖ” never assume consent) + a fire-safe **`trackEvent`** helper (bounded by a timeout, never throws into a feature path). Wired **`workspace_created`** in `workspace.create` as the end-to-end proof site. +8 tests (capture/no-op/sensitivity-throw/no-key/identify + consent resolver). 792 tests; tsc/lint/build/validator clean. **вҡ пёҸ Open decision before full instrumentation (AA1.3):** consent is localStorage-only, so `cookie_consent` rows are usually keyed by `pre_signup_id` not `user_id` вҶ’ server events safely no-op for most users. Needs a consent-propagation mechanism (recommend mirroring the choice into a server-readable cookie; small ADR-0073 amendment) before wiring the remaining ~30 sites. No migration.
- **2026-06-27** вҖ” **feat: AA1.1 вҖ” consent-aware PostHog client provider (ADR-0074).** First slice of the analytics build: a `PostHogProvider` (`posthog-js`) mounted in the `(app)` shell вҖ” the single deliberate **client-side analytics exception** (recorded in ADR-0074 + the lock-in inventory; the SDK can't live behind a server-only adapter). Guarantees: **hard no-op** unless `NEXT_PUBLIC_POSTHOG_KEY` is set (un-provisioned envs never phone home); **consent-gated** (ADR-0073) вҖ” pageviews/autocapture + session replay run **only on "accept all"**, "necessary"/no-choice means no init/opt-out, reacting live to the cookie banner via a new `cookie-consent-changed` event (+ cross-tab `storage`); **never in the participant runtime** (`/take/*`, ADR-0014 вҖ” verified: `posthog-js` absent from the `/take` bundle); session replay **masks all inputs** so researcher-typed content never reaches a recording; client identify deferred (anonymous stable `distinct_id`) to keep PII minimal. Threading: `design/page.tsx` passes filtered `ai-chat` blocks вҶ’ `DesignWorkspace` (passes `themeVars` + `aiBlocks`) вҶ’ `ChatAppearanceEditor`. UI-only, migration-free; 681 vitest green; tsc + lint + build clean.

- **2026-06-22** вҖ” **fix(builder): Replicate is gated to frozen studies, not drafts (ADR-0018).** The Replicate button in the Builder Details panel showed on any study including a brand-new draft, so you could "replicate" a plan (and self-replicate your own draft). - **2026-06-22** вҖ” **fix(studies): study delete failed silently вҖ” comprehensive FK cleanup (root cause: study_presence).** Reproduced it: the real blocker is `study_presence` (ADR-0060) вҖ” the row for *whoever has the study open in the Builder* FK-references it with no on-delete, so "Delete forever" from the Builder always threw, and the mutation had **no `onError`** so the UI showed nothing ("changes saved, nothing happens"). Audited every inbound FK into `experiment`/`experiment_version` and the delete tx now clears all of them in dependency order: `study_presence`, `study_record`, `saved_record`, comments+mentions (by experimentId вҖ” covers block-instance threads, not just study), `quality_flag`вҶ’`payout_record`вҶ’`provider_submission` (before sessions/responses), and nulls `panel_member.source_experiment_id` + `playground_card.converted_study_id`. Added `onError` (alert) so a delete can never fail silently again. +1 regression test (delete a legacy template-clone that has a presence row + block comment). 677 vitest green; tsc + lint + build clean. **Migration-free.**
- **2026-06-22** вҖ” **fix(studies): can't delete a study that was saved as a template.** `studies.delete` didn't clean up `workspace_template` rows that FK-reference the experiment + its frozen version (ON DELETE no action), so deleting a template's source study was blocked ("Delete forever" failed). The delete tx now removes templates `WHERE source_experiment_id = study` first (a template's `source_version_id` is always a version of its `source_experiment_id`, so this covers both FKs) вҖ” the source study + its templates cascade away together. +1 test (delete-source succeeds + removes the template). 676 vitest green; build clean. - **2026-06-04** вҖ” **fix(prod): module picker empty вҖ” webpack `module`-shadow bug.** After confirming the prod catalogue was seeded (8/9), the "Add block" picker stayed empty. A step-through diagnostic (`/api/debugmodules`, now removed) showed `modules.list` throwing `invalid input syntax for type uuid: "12589"` while every other workspace query passed; postgres.js exposed the SQL: `inner join "module" on "module_version"."module_id" = $1` with `$1="12589"` вҖ” the join column had become a bound parameter. Root cause: `modules.ts` imported the Drizzle table as the bare identifier **`module`**, which webpack's CJS module-wrapper param shadows in the minified prod bundle вҶ’ `module.id` resolved to the **numeric webpack module id**, not the column. Prod-only (minification) so dev + 159 vitest all passed; the diagnostic's own namespaced `schema.module.id` returned 9, localising it. **Fix:** renamed export `module` вҶ’ `moduleTable` (DB name `"module"` unchanged) with a footgun comment + updated the 3 importers (`modules.ts`, `seed-core.ts`, `seed.test.ts`); removed the temp endpoint. Typecheck + 13 seed/migration tests + `next build` clean. Full write-up in `06_qa/audit-logs/2026-06-04-v171-polish-deploy.md`. **Guardrail noted:** add a lint rule banning imports named `module`/`exports`/`require`.

- **2026-06-03** вҖ” **feat: V1.7 PR-4 вҖ” cross-workspace forking + Replications + Save & request review (full scope, owner-picked).** Forking was entirely unbuilt (schema columns + `isReplication` flags + badges existed, but no mutation, no affordance, the Replications tab a disabled placeholder), so PR-4 built it. **ADR-0018** decides the cross-tenant read forking requires: one permission-gated `loadForkSource` (forkable iff `forkable_by='public'` OR the caller is an active member of the source workspace; `link-only` deferred) вҖ” the single audited exception to the otherwise-universal workspace scoping. `studies.fork({studyId})` reads the source via that loader, copies its latest runnable (else tip) snapshot + conditions вҖ” block `instanceId`s **preserved** so divergence aligns by identity вҖ” into a new **private** experiment in the caller's workspace with version-pinned lineage (`fork_of_experiment_id` + `fork_of_version_id`), and emits the **`fork`** event (вҶ’ the source author + their Followers; tags copied; best-effort). `studies.setForkable` flips PrivateвҶ”Public-replicable (owner-workspace only); `StudyDetail` now carries `forkableBy` + `ownerId`. `studies.getReplications` returns the **parent** (if this study is a fork) + the **children** (forks of it, cross-tenant), each with a `diffBlocks` divergence **withheld (null)** when the caller can't see the other protocol (not public + not their workspace) вҖ” so private cross-tenant protocols don't leak. `diffBlocks` (pure, in `blocks.ts`) aligns by `instanceId` вҶ’ added/removed/changed/unchanged, ignoring config key order. **UI:** the Builder right-panel **Replications tab** goes live (parent + children + `+/вҲ’/~/=` divergence chips, "divergence hidden" for withheld); the Details panel gains a **Replicate this study** button (вҶ’ routes to the fork) + a **PrivateвҶ”Public-replicable** toggle; and the long-disabled **"Save & request review"** dialog path is enabled вҖ” a reviewer picker (`workspace.members`) вҶ’ `studies.saveAndRequestReview` validates the reviewer is an active member, creates the named version, and emits **`review_request`** (вҶ’ the reviewer in ActivityВ·Yours) + the Follows-only `new_named_version`. **141 vitest green (+8: diffBlocks unit Г—4; same-workspace fork preserves instanceIds + visible diff + parent link; cross-workspace fork FORBIDDEN-private / allowed-public-emits-fork / diff-withheld; saveAndRequestReview emits review_request + non-member BAD_REQUEST); - **2026-06-03** вҖ” **feat: V1.7 PR-2 вҖ” fan-out live + ActivityВ·Yours destination.** The notification fan-out now runs end to end (ADR-0015). `emit()` wired into existing flows: `studies.preregister`вҶ’`preregister_complete` + `studies.saveAsNamed`вҶ’`new_named_version` (both Follows-only вҖ” activity_event, no notification) and the registry-push jobвҶ’`osf_push_complete`, emitted as a **SYSTEM event** (`actorUserId:null`) so the initiator (who is the recipient вҖ” resolveRecipientsвҶ’data.userId) isn't dropped by the actor-exclusion filter; the emit is best-effort (a notify failure never fails the push). The **Activity destination** (`/activity`, activity-destination.md wireframe gate committed first): a thin RSC вҶ’ client `ActivityFeed` with Yours/Follows tabs. **Yours** reads `notifications.list`, renders researcher-native verb phrases per event type ("commented on" / "mentioned you" / "resolved a comment" / "replicated" / "your preregistration вҖҰ is live" + the DOI link), links each row to the study's Share stage, and **on open marks the unread rows read so the rail badge clears** (IA v0.3 В§Notifications вҖ” no bell) while keeping this-visit "new" accents from a first-load snapshot. **Follows** ships its tab with a deferred empty-state (live in PR-3). Left-rail **Activity** activated with an unread-count badge (count paired with an `aria-label`, never color-only). Comment events now denormalize `studyId`+`studyTitle` into their `data` so an Activity row can name + link the study (the notification row stores `data`, not the activity_event's `related`). **129 vitest green (+4: osf_push_complete system-event recipient; the commentвҶ’fan-outвҶ’YoursвҶ’markRead/markAllRead chain with per-user scope; saveAsNamed Follows-only); typecheck + build clean (/activity 2.26 kB).** studies + registry-push test harnesses updated (clear event tables before their FK parents; scope enqueue assertions to registry.push). **Next: PR-3** вҖ” ActivityВ·Follows (`activity_event Г— follow`) + the four `+Follow` affordances.

- **2026-06-02** вҖ” **Commit 3 (feat(auth)): Clerk AuthAdapter + provider + route protection.** `05_app/server/adapters/auth.clerk.ts` implements the `AuthAdapter` against **Clerk v7** and is the only file importing `@clerk/nextjs/server`: `getCurrentUser` maps a Clerk user to our `AuthUser` (primary email lowercased, `displayName` from `fullName`, `avatarUrl`, `hasCompletedOnboarding` from `publicMetadata`) and is null-safe (never throws); `requireCurrentUser` throws a typed `UnauthorizedError`; `getCurrentSession` derives `createdAt`/`expiresAt` from `sessionClaims` `iat`/`exp` (no extra Backend API call); `signOut` revokes the active session via `clerkClient`; `getUserMetadata`/`setUserMetadata` read+write the narrow `publicMetadata` bag (Clerk shallow-merges, so partial patches are safe). `auth.ts` retired the throwing Proxy вҶ’ `auth = clerkAuthAdapter` (the one-line vendor-swap point) and `AuthUserMetadata` gained `hasCompletedOnboarding` so onboarding finalize (commit 4) writes it through the adapter, never importing Clerk in feature code. `app/layout.tsx` wrapped in `<ClerkProvider>`; `middleware.ts` uses `clerkMiddleware` + `createRouteMatcher` to protect the future `/studies`, `/library`, `/frameworks`, `/settings` paths (the `(auth)` pages stay public; route-group folders aren't part of the URL, so the matcher targets real paths). `04_architecture/lock-in-inventory.md`'s Clerk row now records **three deliberate exceptions**, all removed on the ClerkвҶ’Better Auth migration: (1) `<ClerkProvider>` at the layout root, (2) `clerkMiddleware` at the project root, (3) the `(auth)` pages' client hooks (`useSignUp`/`useSignIn`/`useClerk`) вҖ” building custom auth UI (ADR-0007 bans Clerk's prebuilt UI components) requires the client SDK, and the `AuthAdapter` only ever covered server identity. The adapter README's current-adapters table now points `AuthAdapter` at `auth.clerk.ts`. QA: 12 adapter unit tests (happy + auth-fail + field mapping + metadata + signOut, Clerk fully mocked) plus the 9 migration tests = **21 green**; `npm run typecheck` clean; a `grep` confirms no `@clerk` imports leak into feature code (only the two framework exceptions + the adapter folder). - **2026-06-02** вҖ” **Commit 2 (feat(db)): Drizzle bootstrap + first migration.** `05_app/server/db/schema.ts` is the single source of truth for the database shape вҖ” `user` / `workspace` / `member` (data-model 01) + `experiment` / `experiment_version` (data-model 00), five pgEnums (`member_role`, `member_status`, `forkable_by`, `experiment_version_kind`, `amendment_classification`), and every CHECK the data model specifies: experiment fork half-null consistency, `experiment_version` name-required-unless-autosave, the ADR-0004 amendment pair (`supersedes_version_id` + non-empty `change_summary` both set or both null), and `member` status/user consistency; plus unique indexes for one membership per `(workspace, user)` and monotonic `(experiment, version_number)`. The `experiment вҶ” experiment_version` circular FK is resolved with a nullable `current_version_id` + post-create `ALTER TABLE` (drizzle-kit handled it). Driver is **postgres-js** with `prepare:false` (`server/db/client.ts`), **not** `drizzle-orm/neon-http`, because onboarding finalize (commit 4) needs an interactive transaction the HTTP driver can't do. `drizzle.config.ts` loads `.env.local` (drizzle-kit, unlike Next, doesn't auto-load it). The first migration `0000_quiet_vampiro.sql` was generated by drizzle-kit and **applied to the Neon dev DB** (one harmless `NOTICE`: a 63-char FK identifier truncated by Postgres вҖ” deterministic on both generate and apply, so no drift). QA per `qa-and-testing.md`: a hermetic **pglite** migration test (`server/db/__tests__/migration.test.ts`) вҖ” 9 tests green covering forward apply (tables/enums/named CHECKs exist), four constraint-rejection/acceptance cases, and a teardown+reapply idempotency check standing in for "rollback" (drizzle-kit emits no down-migrations; documented in the test). `npm run typecheck` clean. New dev deps: `drizzle-kit`, `dotenv`, `@electric-sql/pglite`, `vitest`; new scripts `db:generate` / `db:migrate` / `test`. Next: commit 3 вҖ” Clerk `AuthAdapter` + `ClerkProvider` + `middleware.ts` + the three lock-in exceptions + adapter unit tests.

- **2026-05-28** вҖ” **Design-language brief вҶ’ v0.5.3.** Stage-tabs placement re-locked from Option A to **Option B** after the project owner saw both visualized side-by-side in chat. Option A (v0.5.2 вҖ” Typeform pattern, stage tabs in top-bar center slot) was familiar but reintroduced a dense full-width band that pulled against the brief's modular-floating-panels spirit. Option B is structurally closer to Miro / FigJam: the page is a board of floating modules and each module owns its own controls; the stage-tabs pill floats over the work surface it controls. Top bar reverts to slim form (workspace chip + breadcrumb on left; вҢҳK + Save when applicable + user avatar on right вҖ” no stage tabs). Stage-tabs pill spans only the center column's width (not the full page) and sits on top of the work surface card with a small internal gutter. Left rail and right context panel cards extend full height of the center column. The reading is now: "three modules on a parchment board вҖ” workspace nav on the left, the study being built in the middle (mode picker on top + work surface beneath), context on the right вҖ” with a slim top hat carrying global chrome above all three." Brief Layout system + Top-bar navigation sections rewritten; `03_design/wireframes/build-stage-builder-mode.md` Layout + Content inventory + Stage-tab-click interaction revised to match. Validator clean (25 instances, no count change вҖ” layout-only revision).
- **2026-05-28** вҖ” **Design-language brief вҶ’ v0.5.2.** Layout-hierarchy correction surfaced by the first wireframe pass. Project owner observed the disconnect between top bar / sidebar and the separate full-width stage-tabs strip: the stage strip stretched above the sidebar in v0.5.1's mockup, but stage tabs are **study-scoped** while the sidebar is **workspace-global**. Adjacent full-width rows implied the same hierarchy level, which is wrong. **Fix (Option A вҖ” Typeform pattern):** stage tabs move into the **top bar's center slot** between breadcrumb (left) and Save (right). Top bar grows in height. Sidebar starts directly below the top bar with no intervening full-width strip. The scope hierarchy becomes spatially literal вҖ” workspace-global chrome (sidebar) is one tier; study-scoped chrome (stage tabs) is nested inside the top bar, not stretched across the sidebar. Top-bar content is now determined by what the breadcrumb points at: on a destination (Studies, Library, etc.) the center slot is empty and the Save button hides; on a study object the center slot carries the six stage tabs (`Build В· Preview В· Share В· Preregister В· Run В· Results`) and Save appears on the right. Updates: brief Layout system + Top-bar navigation sections rewritten; `03_design/wireframes/build-stage-builder-mode.md` Layout + Content inventory + Interactions revised; re-rendered the Builder visualizer Light + Dark side-by-side with the corrected pattern in chat. Validator clean (25 instances; no count change since correction was layout-only).

- **2026-05-28** вҖ” **ADR-0009 accepted** (`04_architecture/adrs/0009-supply-side-strategy.md`). Three-layer hybrid strategy for the biggest non-technical risk: Layer 1 default virtue (architectural posture вҖ” already structurally enabled by ADRs 0001-0007 via schemas-first, immutable versions, asset freeze, preregistration amendments, OSF push; ongoing discipline in product/UX decisions); Layer 2 demand-first V1 GTM (consortia, replicators, open-science labs; explicitly NOT reluctant-author segments); Layer 3 mandate leverage V2+ partnerships (selected journals + funders; gated by V1 product evidence). Explicitly accepts that the back catalogue of un-runnable studies is lost вҖ” flow > stock. Strategic ADR; more posture commitments than code commitments. Validator clean (16 instances).
- **2026-05-28** вҖ” **ADR-0007 accepted** (`04_architecture/adrs/0007-path-a-vs-b.md`). Path A (Vercel + Clerk + Liveblocks + Inngest) with adapter discipline. Four interfaces: `HostingShape`, `AuthAdapter`, `RealtimeAdapter`, `BackgroundJobAdapter`. No vendor-specific types in app code. No Clerk pre-built UI in production. Lock-in inventory at `04_architecture/lock-in-inventory.md` (to be created at Build start) tracks deliberate exceptions; PR review enforces the discipline. Cost-ceiling triggers: $200/mo plan, $500/mo execute, per single managed service. Per-piece migration order: Clerk first (per-MAU pricing makes it worst at scale), then Liveblocks, then Inngest, hosting last. The adapter philosophy is now consistent across infrastructure (this ADR), registries (ADR-0005), AI providers (ADR-0006), and modules (ADR-0001). Validator clean (15 instances).
- **2026-05-28** вҖ” **ADR-0006 accepted** (`04_architecture/adrs/0006-ai-plugin-architecture.md`). Task-based AI architecture per product-brief decision В§2 (V1 architecture-ready, V2+ feature-bearing). Option B: Tasks are first-class typed operations with input/output schemas + prompt templates; AIProviderAdapter interface mirrors RegistryAdapter from ADR-0005; schemas-first validation enforced via ADR-0001's existing module schema infrastructure; per-tenant routing with sensitivity tags (`metadata_only` / `experiment_definition` / `participant_data` / `pii`); append-only `ai_invocation` audit log; per-tenant cost metering (`TenantAIMeter`); caching for deterministic tasks; human-in-the-loop UX default. V1 ships interface + stub adapter + gateway + audit + metering; zero AI features. Four new data-model entities sketched (AIProvider, AIProviderConnection, AIInvocation, TenantAIMeter). Validator clean (14 instances).
- **2026-05-28** вҖ” **ADR-0005 accepted** (`04_architecture/adrs/0005-osf-integration.md`). Push-to-OSF on preregistration via OAuth + Inngest async push. Sub-option B.3: JSON snapshot + rendered PDF + OSF template-field mapping + materials. Per-user OAuth (researchers own their OSF identity), default-on per-registration opt-out, async with retry, failed pushes flag the version without blocking preregistration. **Registry-agnostic adapter interface** so future registries (AsPredicted, ClinicalTrials.gov, PsyArXiv) plug in via the same shape. Amendments push as new OSF registrations referencing the prior DOI. Sketched three new data-model entities (Registry, RegistryConnection, RegistryPush) for a future entry. Validator clean (13 instances).

- **2026-05-28** вҖ” **ADR-0004 accepted** (`04_architecture/adrs/0004-preregistration-amendments.md`). Formalizes how legitimate corrections to immutable preregistered versions work: a new `kind: preregistered` ExperimentVersion with `supersedes_version_id` (FK) + required non-empty `change_summary` + optional `amendment_classification`. Both versions remain public, immutable, queryable. UI shows lineage in both directions. Matches OSF / ClinicalTrials.gov / AsPredicted convention. Three new fields added to ExperimentVersion in `00-core-entities.md`; DB CHECK + app-level constraint specified. ADR queue renumbered: 0005 = OSF integration, 0006 = AI plug-in, 0007 = Path A vs B, 0008 = plugin model. Validator clean (8 instances).
- **2026-05-28** вҖ” **ADR-0003 accepted** (`04_architecture/adrs/0003-asset-storage.md`). Hybrid asset storage: researcher chooses per-asset between internal R2 upload and external link; auto-freeze on preregistration/publication (per-asset opt-out); failed freezes flag the version with `replication_risk: link_only`; content-hash dedup for internal assets; per-tenant storage metering architected (pricing model deferred). Sketched Asset and TenantStorageMeter entities for future data-model entry. Validator clean (7 instances).

Fork is not a separate entity вҖ” it's an Experiment with FKs (explained in doc). Framework + FrameworkVersion sketched briefly as parallel to Experiment. Resolved 5 ADR contradictions: mutable themes vs. immutable versions (theme_snapshot embed); module locks JSON vs. join table (JSON for V1); fork = copy or reference (both, at different layers); cross-tenant forks (allowed, gated by forkable_by); deprecated modules (informational, not refused). - **2026-05-27** вҖ” Added the "Speak researcher, not developer" rule to `00_meta/rules/design-rules.md` with a starter translation table (fork вҶ’ Replicate/Adapt; snapshot вҶ’ Saved version; module вҶ’ Question/Item/Artifact; etc.). - **2026-05-27** вҖ” **ADR-0002 accepted** (`04_architecture/adrs/0002-forking-model.md`). Adopted stripped Option B: snapshot-based forking with pull-from-upstream deferred but forward-ready. Eight load-bearing principles: immutable version history per experiment; versions have a kind (autosave / named / preregistered / published); every version captures the full module-version lock set (per ADR-0001); forks reference a specific parent version, not an experiment in the abstract; forks are fully editable after creation; participant data never copied across forks; public-forkable default with per-experiment opt-out; frameworks share the model. Includes an 8-item forward-readiness checklist so upgrade to full B (pull-from-upstream, eventually merge-back) is feature-add, not migration. Validator clean (3 instances).
- **2026-05-27** вҖ” **ADR-0001 accepted** (`04_architecture/adrs/0001-modular-composition-theme-overlays.md`). Adopted versioned modular composition with theme overlays (Option C from the chat discussion). Five load-bearing principles: module identity is `source/key@version`; module schemas are first-class (Zod/JSON Schema); themes are pure-functional overlays (filter/configure, never mutate); forks reference module versions explicitly; module registry interface is plugin-ready (deferred plugin runtime). Module granularity = question type / artifact; blocks are compositions; frameworks are curated content. Calibration: project owner explicitly chose architectural flexibility + data safety + fork integrity over time-to-ship. Validator clean (2 instances).
- **2026-05-27** вҖ” Resolved 6 key product decisions in `02_product/product-brief.md`: positioning is "Qualtrics + GitHub for research" (combination is the wedge); thematic spaces are composable overlays on one everything-space (NOT separate products); AI is V1-architecture-ready / V2+ feature-bearing; chatbot surveys are V2 conversational rendering; curation is human (project owner); stats are narrow (G\*Power + manipulation-check + quick dashboard descriptives); AI synthesis is extraction (procedure + materials) not full generation. Reordered the ADR queue вҖ” ADR-0001 is now the modular composition / theme overlay model, the load-bearing decision.
